However, once the automatic curtains are opened, the floor-to-ceiling glass windows are very dirty and affect the view. The swimming pool is not built in the hotel, but is in the swimming pool on the left side of the door. The facilities and breakfast are average. For dinner, we went to Primus opposite. Except for the fact that there was someone at the door who opened the door and took the initiative to help with luggage, and the front desk had a good attitude, the overall situation was very average. I don't know how it ranked among the top three in Luoyang. In addition, the hotel's new toothpaste turned black when opened! msg:Let's start with the conclusion: This is a 102-point check-in experience. If you love love, you must choose him when you come to Luoyang!
1. The room type will be upgraded for free as soon as we check in, and the favorability will instantly upup
2. The upgraded American lake view room, the room is spacious and clean, and the layout is very simple, which is what we like. The oversized double bed faces the Yading Lake, which makes people feel very comfortable. The toilet separates dry and wet, and there is a special dressing table (light and suitable for makeup).
3. The service staff was super caring. They watched us wash our clothes, sent us laundry detergent separately, watched us use the computer, gave us a computer stand and mouse pad, and gave us a spare battery card to facilitate computer charging. I have never seen it. I was so touched by such a caring hotel.
4. Breakfast is also top-notch. My husband and I had two bowls of raw porridge for two days, and we didn't drank enough. All kinds of self-service ingredients are also readily available.
5. In fact, the most important thing in the hotel is the soft power of the service, which makes the guests feel at home. The Aden Hotel is the best hotel I have ever stayed in. From the front desk staff to the cleaning service staff to the restaurant staff, they are all enthusiastic. It really makes people feel good about it, even with a good impression of the city of Luoyang.
